< Text>
Authentic Japanese cuisine.  If you miss Japan Town choices in San Francisco, you will be pleased to have found Matsuyama.  Their BentoBaku offerings are really good,  And, I recommend the Tonkatsu Pork.  The prices are surprisingly low.  If you miss eating good Japanese food ,  you may not be overy enthusiastic but you won't be sadly disappointed either.  Don't forget, we are in Discovery Bay and it's not likely that the population here of Japanese and Japanese descendants is very high. I, for one, am glad they are here.</Text>

<pictures>None</pictures><userid>100414208214591308416</userid><response>None<//response><Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
This is a fantastic store for throwaway items. Seasonal little accents and accessories, stuff for kids, stuff for single use. You name it, they got it.

Obviously, unless you have serious financial constraints and you need an item NOW, this isn't the place to shop for long lasting, high quality things. However, they come in really handy when you're in a bind. I needed a strainer, bought it here for a buck, used it that day, washed it, and it was rusted within a few days.

This place shines for one-time use, disposable, or seasonal items. I've bought a boat-load of seasonal accents and party supplies here, and saved a ton of money doing it.

The only reason for the 4 stars instead of 5 is that every time I go in, the store is a complete mess, especially in the front, where they have carts full of returns piled up.< /review>
